import datetime

class AccountData:
    def __init__(self, b, id, status):
        self.b = b  # balance
        self.id = id
        self.status = status

class Logger:
    def log(self, msg):
        print(f"LOG: {msg}")

class TransactionManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = Logger()

    
    
    def do_stuff(self, p1, p2, p3, p4, p5, p6):
      
        # Check if source is valid and has money
   
        if p1.b > p3 and p1.status != "LOCKED":
            
            # check if user is allowed to do this
   
            if (p5 == "ADMIN") or (p5 == "USER" and p3 < 5000) or (p5 == "SUPER" and p6 == False):
                
                # perform the transfer
   
                p1.b = p1.b - p3 
                p2.b = p2.b + p3 
                
                # calculate tax
   
                t_val = p3 * 0.05
                if p6:
                    t_val = p3 * 0.12
                
                final_deduction = p3 + t_val
                
   
                rslt = f"Trans {p4}: {p1.id} moved {p3} to {p2.id}. Fee: {t_val}"
                
                # log the result
                self.logger.log(rslt)
                
                # update timestamp
   
                now = datetime.datetime.now()
                print(f"Executed at: {now.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
                
                return True
            else:
                # user should be authorized
   
                print("Error: Unauthorized")
                return False
        else:
            print("Error: Insufficient funds or locked")
            return False

# --- Execution ---
source = AccountData(10000, "ACC-01", "SAVINGS")
dest = AccountData(500, "ACC-02", "CHECKING")
mgr = TransactionManager()


mgr.do_stuff(source, dest, 1000, "TXN-99", "USER", False) ^qynJpvzb

import datetime

class HourlyWorker:
    def __init__(self, name, id, rate, hours):
        self.worker_name = name
        self.id_number = id
        self.hourly_rate = rate
        self.time_logged = hours

    def get_total_payout(self):
        
        # Step 1: Calculate Gross
        gross = self.hourly_rate * self.time_logged
        
        
        tax_amount = 0
        if gross > 5000:
            tax_amount = gross * 0.2
        else:
            tax_amount = gross * 0.1
            
        final = gross - tax_amount
        
        # Step 3: Format and Log
        print(f"--- PAYSLIP ---")
        print(f"Employee: {self.worker_name}")
        print(f"Amount: {final}")
        print(f"Date: {datetime.datetime.now()}")
        return final

class SalaryWorker:
    def __init__(self, name, emp_id, annual_salary):
        self.full_name = name
        self.emp_id = emp_id
        self.annual_salary = annual_salary

    def process_monthly_pay(self):
        
        # Step 1: Calculate Gross
        monthly_gross = self.annual_salary / 12
        
        # Step 2: Tax Logic 
        t = 0
        if monthly_gross > 5000:
            t = monthly_gross * 0.2
        else:
            t = monthly_gross * 0.1
            
        net = monthly_gross - t
        
        # Step 3: Format and Log
        print(f"--- PAYSLIP ---")
        print(f"Employee: {self.full_name}")
        print(f"Amount: {net}")
        print(f"Date: {datetime.datetime.now()}")
        return net ^HsqtZgqW
